**1. Garis Kepemimpinan (Imamah):**

*   **Sunni:** Kepemimpinan setelah Nabi Muhammad SAW dipilih melalui musyawarah (konsensus) atau penunjukan. Khalifah pertama adalah Abu Bakar [alkhoirot](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQEE12V4B2Vvjm5x8gs5uFhMzBUcnMxpnOCMY53wvZtU4-ai_Zzfne1fQyzmBssY6XKlrpbpM831AQcsjjWiAtLDxagJC2IDUpmcjyDV-2e0B6d0NMommdD1dOsA_AXiHPne81DvnTE3OzzT7Pw=).
*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah (Twelver):** Meyakini bahwa kepemimpinan (Imamah) adalah hak Ali bin Abi Thalib dan keturunannya melalui penunjukan langsung dari Nabi Muhammad SAW [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFX3Exm29aRfPy3bZWmwtIMlT4-YkbrXEkrUuRB46K6UB24XHnevLJxYzqMOL7WDxTu_4B_A4MqFijlslcYr5whTeoM7OztrK4Dszn24CTIqtUgtXSyeMplVGQ5e_iOcn5D_gFNJV0y6oD2Ogt5f2AKtS6LB9ZXn63QboPHR4cMvfbtcayNHpd1c0BXnk48wj3fzRue9RJbJX-sNR0run--aW_rgZmOBjKn). Mereka percaya pada 12 Imam yang maksum (bebas dari dosa dan kesalahan). Imam pertama adalah Ali bin Abi Thalib, dan Imam terakhir, Muhammad al-Mahdi, diyakini masih hidup dan akan muncul kembali [iuqibogor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHjEYtXTmLVNRO-0O6GyfJcytOCuiRRUUBSAJrxtGL9iiR51NXW6GZYrkqE6-OKkz_zArlKfndM9RYWeUTTe6FEwSXhDID2KCdVStYuG6wYCjTo-EGOd4nh73wNDjJkOWVuFeJE5AF9rVTxz1DC0TK9a3HkjnxFPJHZQysWhpjIsYUynZa0x69h). Syiah Itsna'asyariyah meyakini adanya dua belas Imam yang merupakan pemimpin yang sah setelah Nabi Muhammad. Imam pertama adalah Ali bin Abi Thalib, diikuti oleh Hasan dan Husain (cucu Nabi), dan seterusnya hingga Imam ke-12, Muhammad al-Mahdi, yang diyakini berada dalam keadaan gaib dan akan kembali pada akhir zaman [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGkVLg4OUEAdMm8MBdTMotdcFxI1VhRbQ6EwE9qlGfyvoAoZds3PM5YQfX2EjbW8UVERRHKO8-fFuszz-lmAjo16iPkL1gNC2dVlqFKJwuNATbfO2hUbCn1f9a_wJKPhPrgg_yIWn6vyy6mJYS4ycf37XF5El4r2TlxqUxNHYrKf35i8WjGKbKjK59l7xrV_cBhmpmMDPfv5mdzbr8w) [biblehub](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFRQ3ufZOXfpU0Vw16nmEHvsWzAyMwq4nlFer0i2aHm-ttiBePSvT4ue5Gg4odFCPJ6zUyW49GdcnmqbnGO6FDxHHltmSdNMfdovvmF1tub62rI9M6n5eMPSQLtMFMx2O9lmcsVGQKbUGPjSmKC7PiB8G3ygmAol60=).
*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Tidak percaya bahwa Imamah ditunjuk secara ilahi. Mereka percaya bahwa setiap keturunan Ali (Alid) dapat menjadi Imam jika dia bangkit melawan ketidakadilan [iuqibogor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHjEYtXTmLVNRO-0O6GyfJcytOCuiRRUUBSAJrxtGL9iiR51NXW6GZYrkqE6-OKkz_zArlKfndM9RYWeUTTe6FEwSXhDID2KCdVStYuG6wYCjTo-EGOd4nh73wNDjJkOWVuFeJE5AF9rVTxz1DC0TK9a3HkjnxFPJHZQysWhpjIsYUynZa0x69h). Tidak seperti Itsna'asyariyah, Zaidiyah tidak meyakini kemaksuman Imam. Setelah Imam Ali, Imam Hasan, Imam Husain, Imam Ali Zainal Abidin, dan Zaid bin Ali, tanggung jawab imamah diemban oleh laki-laki dari keturunan Fatimah yang memenuhi kriteria: menyeru umat untuk mengakui ke-imamahannya, adil secara dhahir, alim, pemberani, dan dibaiat oleh orang-orang mukmin untuk berjihad [wikishia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQEJO5-hTpcLsNAXgAjopRFDfIJPzRTZ6waBnAT6H-3f3Z1B-pn929YMOtcxi1YUCXBSO317h_oTQtihyZ6laVWeZYHNSzwph7R9t0qyfHZ0pSIsWTkR1KKyL9VeJL8tm2E=).

**2. Konsep Imamah:**

*   **Sunni:** Tidak memiliki konsep Imamah seperti dalam Syiah. Pemimpin dipilih berdasarkan kemampuan dan dukungan komunitas.
*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Imam memiliki otoritas spiritual yang setara dengan Nabi dan merupakan penafsir agama yang tidak mungkin salah. Imam diangkat secara ilahi dan maksum [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFX3Exm29aRfPy3bZWmwtIMlT4-YkbrXEkrUuRB46K6UB24XHnevLJxYzqMOL7WDxTu_4B_A4MqFijlslcYr5whTeoM7OztrK4Dszn24CTIqtUgtXSyeMplVGQ5e_iOcn5D_gFNJV0y6oD2Ogt5f2AKtS6LB9ZXn63QboPHR4cMvfbtcayNHpd1c0BXnk48wj3fzRue9RJbJX-sNR0run--aW_rgZmOBjKn).
*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Imam adalah pemimpin yang saleh dan berani yang bangkit melawan ketidakadilan, tetapi mereka tidak harus maksum atau ditunjuk secara ilahi.

**3. Sumber Hukum:**

*   **Sunni:** Menggunakan Al-Quran dan Hadis (perkataan dan perbuatan Nabi Muhammad SAW) yang diriwayatkan oleh para sahabat Nabi secara luas [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFX3Exm29aRfPy3bZWmwtIMlT4-YkbrXEkrUuRB46K6UB24XHnevLJxYzqMOL7WDxTu_4B_A4MqFijlslcYr5whTeoM7OztrK4Dszn24CTIqtUgtXSyeMplVGQ5e_iOcn5D_gFNJV0y6oD2Ogt5f2AKtS6LB9ZXn63QboPHR4cMvfbtcayNHpd1c0BXnk48wj3fzRue9RJbJX-sNR0run--aW_rgZmOBjKn) [tempo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbDyQnBXyR8sVNwbvY1-Z8XRNKbZ_-M-tZSockappnSaqoWCHeDYrCKuvzrBWzSiy48ZkcV5bqrm8MeI44gpkpA6WD1BdVFNHjP_CT9h8c4r9xr2EY2EQhfWZq8juIaGnxDW9o47txJ3qZOxl8hq6kT2EYAa3a9yq5Yb05hlm2hLMLIOM=).
*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Menggunakan Al-Quran dan Hadis yang diriwayatkan oleh Ahlul Bait (keluarga Nabi), yaitu Ali, Fatimah, Hasan, Husain, dan keturunan mereka.
*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Menggunakan Al-Quran, Hadis, dan akal (rasionalisme) dalam menetapkan hukum. Mereka tidak membatasi penerimaan hadis hanya dari keluarga Nabi, tetapi juga menerima riwayat dari sahabat Nabi lainnya [tempo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbDyQnBXyR8sVNwbvY1-Z8XRNKbZ_-M-tZSockappnSaqoWCHeDYrCKuvzrBWzSiy48ZkcV5bqrm8MeI44gpkpA6WD1BdVFNHjP_CT9h8c4r9xr2EY2EQhfWZq8juIaGnxDW9o47txJ3qZOxl8hq6kT2EYAa3a9yq5Yb05hlm2hLMLIOM=).

**4. Pandangan terhadap Sahabat Nabi:**

*   **Sunni:** Menghormati semua sahabat Nabi Muhammad SAW dan menganggap mereka sebagai orang-orang yang adil dan dapat dipercaya.
*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Beberapa kelompok Syiah Imamiyah dan Ismailiyah memiliki pandangan yang sangat kritis terhadap para sahabat Nabi yang tidak mendukung Ali sebagai khalifah pertama.
*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Memiliki pandangan yang lebih lunak terhadap para sahabat Nabi [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGgD8Z09Osj7rwy2UB6-dDgUMfDJdvs125DXbBEDbP_ShDHIrYvy69nPuvJVUS64XGh80z1LHKt_0XRhAaiXbTZkMNHew5cCP2EA9lmS1-O1GtWaz7Tzlj_NRZZ6Z5Ofk_bbefioP0x5iL77VhOgdqtX2d4ehueb_Ce0H5eZJVLdwx2Y6yQf9bXRwJNhRuW-Gx6aRKZcGgTQoXb43VP). Mereka mengakui Abu Bakar, Umar, dan Utsman sebagai khalifah yang sah, meskipun mereka meyakini bahwa Ali lebih utama [tempo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbDyQnBXyR8sVNwbvY1-Z8XRNKbZ_-M-tZSockappnSaqoWCHeDYrCKuvzrBWzSiy48ZkcV5bqrm8MeI44gpkpA6WD1BdVFNHjP_CT9h8c4r9xr2EY2EQhfWZq8juIaGnxDW9o47txJ3qZOxl8hq6kT2EYAa3a9yq5Yb05hlm2hLMLIOM=).

**5. Taqiyyah (Disimulasi):**

*   **Sunni:** Tidak mengenal konsep taqiyyah dalam keadaan normal.
*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Membolehkan taqiyyah (menyamarkan keyakinan) untuk melindungi diri dari penganiayaan.
*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Menolak taqiyyah.

**6. Keyakinan Tambahan:**

*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Memiliki rukun iman yang disebut Ushuluddin, yang terdiri dari Tauhid (keesaan Allah), Adl (keadilan Allah), Nubuwwah (kenabian), Imamah (kepemimpinan), dan Ma'ad (hari kebangkitan) [jurnal-maarifinstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQEhZqsUZ29UsslLrEymGPwzN22F_dIdL7yQ5-KEh3sxC5EXD23dNbQ5TKJbprLquXhkENmAiF5VPsqCoGAr6lfuClO6eAr0eoBhhO5M1A2kXEEu7h0zv1_TLzTwL6qMM0erd0mQwrAjaFmYIXrDoj3TUjcvNXMtwywymFZHCs5Ej_VQREwOeRZcapk=).
*   **Sunni:** Rukun Iman ada 6 (enam) :Iman kepada Allah, Iman kepada Malaikat-malaikat Nya, Iman kepada Kitab-kitab Nya, Iman kepada Rasul Nya, Iman kepada Yaumil Akhir / hari kiamat, Iman kepada Qadar, baik-buruknya dari Allah [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF8mUGgP_k5tVOMi-SY2mY7T-X6ELM2YKfQ1fFjmfvfEzzWioOlhJf9uUwuMVk4LxLd_8SgMQnHzxZOx2l8nh6D8sJ-7Vxpd6bXxRLKg_u6PzsmUipHN98W2HvV6uQhgcObfEwX0WzPlMFfARvGlhUQVMmKUFJZupFzz4aWPPeMFT2X7P16ZoFi_PSlQzQ05KELlWQuABxAq5bMQTWOVESO8HD6-g==).
*   **Syiah:** Rukun Islam Syiah juga ada 5 (lima) tapi berbeda: a) As-Sholah, b) As-Shoum, c) Az-Zakah, d) Al-Haj, e) Al wilayah [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF8mUGgP_k5tVOMi-SY2mY7T-X6ELM2YKfQ1fFjmfvfEzzWioOlhJf9uUwuMVk4LxLd_8SgMQnHzxZOx2l8nh6D8sJ-7Vxpd6bXxRLKg_u6PzsmUipHN98W2HvV6uQhgcObfEwX0WzPlMFfARvGlhUQVMmKUFJZupFzz4aWPPeMFT2X7P16ZoFi_PSlQzQ05KELlWQuABxAq5bMQTWOVESO8HD6-g==).

Berikut adalah rangkuman mengenai sejarah dan doktrin Syiah Zaidiyah berdasarkan hasil pencarian Google:

**Sejarah Syiah Zaidiyah:**

*   **Asal-Usul:** Syiah Zaidiyah dinisbatkan kepada Zaid bin Ali Zainal Abidin, cucu dari Husain bin Ali bin Abi Thalib. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) Ia lahir pada 79 H dan wafat terbunuh pada 122 H. (AnnajahSidogiri.id, 2024-06-18) [annajahsidogiri](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)
*   **Pendirian Mazhab:** Mazhab ini didirikan oleh Imam Zaid bin Ali Zainal Abidin, seorang ahli tafsir, hadis, dan hukum Islam. [maryamsejahtera](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) (Mukaddam, Fadhil, & Nor, 2023)
*   **Kemunculan:** Aliran ini muncul dalam tubuh mazhab Syiah pada tahun-tahun pertama abad ke-2 H/ke-8 M. (wikishia, 2024-06-15) Syiah Zaidiyah muncul pada tahun 94 H setelah wafatnya Ali Zainal Abidin. (Ali al-Ghurabi, 1985) [stainh](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-3)
*   **Perkembangan Awal:** Setelah wafatnya Ali Zainal Abidin, kelompok Syiah terbagi menjadi pengikut Zaid bin Ali dan Muhammad al-Baqir. (Ali al-Ghurabi, 1985) [stainh](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-3)
*   **Pusat Pemerintahan:**
    *   **Yaman:** Pusat pemerintahan Zaidiyah Yaman berada di Sha'dah. [wikishia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4) Mazhab ini secara resmi disebarkan oleh Yahya bin Husain bin Qasim. [wikishia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4) Pemerintahan Zaidiyah di Yaman berlangsung hingga tahun 1960. [wikishia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4) (wikishia, 2024-06-15)
    *   **Iran:** Pemerintahan Zaidiyah di Iran berdiri di Tabarestan dan Dailaman, didirikan oleh Hasan bin Zaid dan berlangsung hingga tahun 316 H. (wikishia, 2024-06-15) [wikishia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
*   **Pengaruh di Yaman:** Sekte Zaidiyah telah lama mengakar di Yaman sejak Yahya Hamiduddin memisahkan Yaman dari kekuasaan Turki dan mendirikan negara Zaidiyah hingga tahun 1962. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5) (Hidayatullah.com, 2015-04-14) Saat ini sekitar 45 persen penduduk Yaman bermazhab Zaidiyah. (wikishia, 2024-06-15)
*   **Al-Hautsi:** Para keturunan Badruddin menjadi pemimpin kelompok Al Hautsi dalam melawan pemerintah Yaman. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5) (Hidayatullah.com, 2015-04-14) [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5)

**Doktrin Syiah Zaidiyah:**

*   **Imamah:**
    *   Setelah Imam Ali, Imam Hasan, Imam Husain, Imam Ali Zainal Abidin, dan Zaid bin Ali, tanggung jawab imamah diemban oleh laki-laki dari keturunan Fatimah yang memenuhi kriteria: menyeru umat untuk mengakui ke-imamahannya, adil secara dhahir, alim, pemberani, dan dibaiat oleh orang-orang mukmin untuk berjihad. [wikishia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4) (wikishia, 2024-06-15)
    *   Tidak seperti Syiah lainnya, Zaidiyah tidak menganggap para imam lebih mulia dari Rasulullah ﷺ. Mereka juga tidak menganggap derajat dan keutamaan para imam yang dua belas melebihi para utusan Allah ﷻ. Mes [annajahsidogiri](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)kipun demikian, mereka tetap mengklaim bahwa Ali adalah yang paling utama setelah wafatnya Rasulullah ﷺ. (Anna [annajahsidogiri](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)jahSidogiri.id, 2024-06-18)
    * [annajahsidogiri](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)   Syi'ah Zaidiyah berkeyakinan bahwa pengganti Ali Zainal Abidin adalah Zaid bin Ali (bukan Muhammad al-Baqir). Sekte ini juga berpendapat bahwa Imamah memerlukan pengakuan. (Sant [anfa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6)alia, 2024)
*   **Teologi:** Dalam masalah teologi, Zaidiyah dekat dengan pemikiran Muktazilah, meskipun tidak sepenuhnya sama. Liter [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7)atur teologis Zaidiyah menekankan keadilan dan tanggung jawab manusia serta implikasi politiknya. (Wiki [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7)pedia bahasa Indonesia)
*   * [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8)*Fiqih:** Fikih Zaidiyah merupakan fikih yang paling mirip dengan Ibadi. (Wiki [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7)pedia bahasa Indonesia) Dalam menetapkan hukum, mereka banyak menggunakan mazhab yang beraliran Ahlussunnah wal Jamaah, yaitu Imam Abu Hanifah. (Muka [maryamsejahtera](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2)ddam, Fadhil, & Nor, 2023)
*   **Kitab Rujukan:** Kitab-kitab/referensi Mazhab Zaidiyah yaitu Al-Majmu' yang disusun oleh Zaid bin Ali bin Husein, al-Bahr az-Zahkhar al-Jami' li Mazahib Ulama al-Amsar, dan kitab al-Raud an-Nadir yang merupakan syarah dari al-Majmu'. (Muka [maryamsejahtera](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2)ddam, Fadhil, & Nor, 2023)
*   **Pandangan tentang Sahabat Nabi:**
    *   Umumnya kelompok Syiah menempatkan Khalifah Abu Bakar dan Umar sebagai perampas kekuasaan, tetapi Imam Zaid menentang pendapat tersebut. (Hida [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0)yatullah.com, 2019-01-02)
    *   Kelompok Jarudiyyah (dalam Zaidiyah) menghindari untuk mengkafirkan para sahabat, meskipun mereka menganggap para sahabat telah salah karena gagal mengakui Ali sebagai Khalifah yang sah dan menolak legitimasi Abu Bakar, Umar dan Utsman. (Wiki [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7)pedia bahasa Indonesia)
*   * [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8)*Kemiripan dengan Ahlussunnah:** Syiah Zaidiyah dianggap sebagai golongan yang paling dekat dengan pemahaman Ahlussunnah wal Jamaah atau paling moderat dibandingkan golongan Syiah lainnya. (Anna [annajahsidogiri](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)jahSidogiri.id, 2024-06-18)

**Pe [annajahsidogiri](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)rbedaan dengan Syiah Lain:**

*   **Imamiyah dan Ismailiyah:** Sekte Imamiyah terkenal dengan kepercayaannya terkait kepemimpinan umat Islam yang dipimpin oleh dua belas Imam. Sekte [anfa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-9) [maryamsejahtera](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [anfa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6) Ismailiyah meyakini adanya rangkaian imam yang tidak terputus dengan Ismai'il bin Ja'far yang bertindak sebagai imam ketujuh. (Sant [anfa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-9) [anfa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6)alia, 2024)
*   **Doktrin:** Syiah Zaidiyah memiliki pemahaman yang unik terkait doktrin, praktek keagamaan dan kepemimpinan dibandingkan dengan Syiah Imamiyah dan Ismailiyah. (Santalia, 2024)

**Catatan:**

*   Beberapa sumber menyatakan bahwa meskipun Syiah Zaidiyah lebih moderat, tetap terdapat perbedaan mendasar dengan Ahlussunnah wal Jamaah, terutama dalam hal imamah. (VOA ISLAM, 2015-11-03)
*   Penting untuk tidak menggeneralisasi semua kelompok Syiah sebagai sesat, karena terdapat perbedaan internal yang signifikan. (MENYELISIK POSISI SYIAH DI DALAM ISLAM, 2023-12-03)

Okay, I will conduct targeted Google Searches to gather the most recent, credible information on "Sejarah dan doktrin Syiah Itsna'asyariyah" and synthesize it into a verifiable text artifact.
Syiah Itsna'asyariyah, juga dikenal sebagai Imamiyah atau Twelver Shi'ism, adalah cabang terbesar dari Islam Syiah, meliputi sekitar 85-90% dari seluruh Muslim Syiah. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) Istilah "Itsna'asyariyah" mengacu pada kepercayaan para pengikutnya terhadap dua belas pemimpin yang ditunjuk secara ilahi, yang dikenal sebagai Dua Belas Imam, dan keyakinan mereka bahwa Imam terakhir, Imam al-Mahdi, hidup dalam kegaiban (ghayba) dan akan muncul kembali sebagai "Mahdi yang ditunggu" (al-Mahdi al-muntazar). [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)

**Sejarah Kemunculan dan Perkembangan:**

*   **Awal Mula:** Syiah muncul pada dekade-dekade awal setelah wafatnya Nabi Muhammad SAW pada tahun 632 M. Pemicu utama perpecahan dari tradisi Islam lainnya adalah pertanyaan tentang suksesi yang sah. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [biblehub](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) Syiah meyakini bahwa kepemimpinan umat Muslim seharusnya berada di tangan keluarga Muhammad, khususnya Ali bin Abi Thalib, sepupu dan menantu Nabi. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Perkembangan Doktrin:** Doktrin Syiah Itsna Asyariyah terus berkembang seiring waktu. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [biblehub](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) Konsep dua belas Imam secara resmi berkembang setelah kematian Ja'far al-Sadiq, Imam keenam, pada tahun 765 M. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Pengaruh Politik:** Syiah Itsna Asyariyah memiliki pengaruh signifikan dalam sejarah politik Islam. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) Pada masa lalu, dinasti Safawi menjadikan Syiah Itsna Asyariyah sebagai agama negara di Persia pada tahun 1502 M, yang membedakannya dari kerajaan-kerajaan Sunni lainnya seperti Ottoman. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) Revolusi Iran tahun 1979 juga sangat dipengaruhi oleh ideologi Syiah. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)

**Doktrin-Doktrin Utama:**

*   **Imamah:** Konsep Imamah adalah inti dari ajaran Syiah. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) Mereka meyakini bahwa setelah Nabi Muhammad SAW wafat, kepemimpinan umat Islam harus berada di tangan Ali bin Abi Thalib dan keturunannya. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [biblehub](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) Para Imam dipandang sebagai penerus spiritual dan politik Nabi Muhammad yang ditunjuk secara ilahi, memiliki pengetahuan khusus, dan tidak mungkin berbuat salah (maksum). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Dua Belas Imam:** Syiah Itsna Asyariyah meyakini adanya dua belas Imam yang merupakan pemimpin yang sah setelah Nabi Muhammad. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [stikes-ibnusina](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) Imam pertama adalah Ali bin Abi Thalib, diikuti oleh Hasan dan Husain (cucu Nabi), dan seterusnya hingga Imam ke-12, Muhammad al-Mahdi, yang diyakini berada dalam keadaan gaib dan akan kembali pada akhir zaman. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [biblehub](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2)
*   **Ushuluddin (Lima Rukun Iman):** Dalam hal akidah, Syiah memiliki lima rukun iman yang disebut Ushuluddin: Tauhid (keesaan Allah), Adl (keadilan Allah), Nubuwwah (kenabian), Imamah (kepemimpinan), Ma'ad (hari kebangkitan). [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Ismah (Infallibility):** Konsep Ismah adalah keyakinan bahwa Nabi Muhammad SAW, para nabi lainnya, dan para Imam terbebas dari kesalahan dan dosa. [miraheze](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Taqiyya (Prudent Concealment):** Konsep Taqiyya adalah tindakan menyembunyikan keyakinan seseorang karena takut akan penganiayaan. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)

**Perbedaan dengan Sunni:**

[neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Sumber Hukum:** Selain Al-Quran dan Sunnah Nabi, Syiah juga menjadikan perkataan dan perbuatan para Imam sebagai sumber hukum. [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)

--- Research Result 4 ---
The Sunni and Shia branches of Islam, while sharing core beliefs, differ in legal and ritual practices, particularly concerning prayer, marriage, and inheritance. These differences stem from historical and political disagreements, as well as varying interpretations of Islamic law (Sharia). [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)

### Prayer [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)

*   **Frequency:** Sunni Muslims typically pray five times a day at five distinct times, while Shia Muslims may combine certain prayers, praying three times a day (combining the noon and afternoon prayers, as well as the evening and night prayers). [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)
*   **Physical Postures:** During prayer, Sunni Muslims often place their hands on their chest or stomach in the standing position, whereas Shia Muslims usually keep their hands at their sides. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)
*   **Prostration:** Shia Muslims often place a small piece of clay or soil (turba) on the ground to prostrate on during their prayers, a practice not common among Sunni Muslims.
*   **Recitation:** While both groups recite the opening chapter of the Quran (Al-Fatiha), there may be variations in additional supplications and phrases included in their prayers.
*   **Intercession:** Major groups of Sunnis do not accept intercession. [calloflove](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4) Shia Muslims believe intercessory prayers can be made to Muhammad, his daughter Fatima, and the Twelve Imams. [calloflove](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4)

### Marriage [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3) [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)

*   **Witnesses:** Sunni marriages require two adult male witnesses at the time of the Nikah (marriage contract). [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) Shia marriages do not require witnesses at the time of the Nikah but require them at the time of divorce. [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)
*   **Guardianship:** In Sunni law, there is a long list of guardians for marriage besides the father and grandfather. [lawnotes](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6) Under Shia law, only the father and grandfather can act as legal guardians (Wali-ul-nikah).
*   **Marriage Types:** Sunni law divides marriages into valid, invalid, and irregular (voidable) marriages, while Shia law recognizes only valid or void marriages. [lawcolumn](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7)
*   **Temporary Marriage (Mut'ah):** Shia Muslims believe in Nikah al-Mut'ah (temporary marriage), which is a fixed-term marriage contract that can be renewed, but automatically dissolves once the contract expires. [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) Sunni Muslims do not recognize this type of marriage. [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) Some Sunnis have Nikah-e-Misyar, which is a non-traditional temporary marriage contract, but both Sunni and Shia Muslims disagree over Nikah al Mut'ah and Nikah e Misyar. [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)
*   **Inter-sect Marriage:** It is permissible for a Shi'ite man to marry a Sunni girl if he is from among the moderate Shi'a groups. [dar-alifta](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-8) However, marriage between a Sunni and a Shi'ite is subject to environmental, social, and intellectual considerations. [dar-alifta](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-8)

### Inheritance [wassiyyah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9) [islamicwillstrust](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10)

*   **Classification of Heirs:** The root of the differing Sunni and Shia interpretations of inheritance law lies in heirs' fundamental classification. [pravasitax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-11)
*   **Exclusion of Heirs:** Under Sunni law, the nearest in degree will exclude those related to a deceased by more remote. [wassiyyah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9) Shiaa follows the same, but the outcome of this rule is quite different.
*   **Presence of Daughters:** The Sunni rules allow the Full Brothers or Paternal Brothers to inherit in Daughters' presence, but Shia law completely excludes Full or Paternal Brothers and Paternal Sisters in the presence of Daughters. [wassiyyah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9)
*   **Non-Muslim Inheritors:** Sunni and Shia laws differ in their interpretations and applications of Non-Muslim inheritors. [wassiyyah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9) [ipleaders](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-12)
*   **Distribution:** Sunni law follows the Quranic Law which is the amalgamation of the old customary Law, whereas Shia refuses to believe saying that this law was not endorsed by the Quran itself and therefore new laws must be introduced. [islamicwillstrust](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10)
*   **Heirs:** Sunni law has three classes of heirs: sharers, residuaries, and distant kindred. Shia law has two classes of heirs: shares and residuaries. [ipleaders](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-12)
*   **Doctrine of Primogeniture:** The doctrine of primogeniture is not recognized in Sunni law. [lawnotes](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6) The doctrine of primogeniture is recognized in Shia law.
*   **Per Capita vs. Per Stirpes Distribution:** Under Sunni law, if a person dies leaving three grandsons by a predeceased son and two grandsons by another predeceased son, all five grandsons will inherit the property in equal shares each taking 1/5th share (Per Capita distribution). [pravasitax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-11) Under Shia law, the three children of one predeceased son take 1/2 and other 1/2 goes to the two children of the predeceased son (Per Stirpes distribution). [pravasitax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-11)

It is important to note that both Sunni and Shia Muslims share the same fundamental beliefs and practices of Islam, including the five pillars. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) The Quran does not explicitly mention Shia or Sunni Islam because the division occurred after its revelation. [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-13) The divisions that arose between them are historical and political rather than religiously mandated. [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-13)


--- Research Result 5 ---
The theological differences between Sunni and Shia Islam manifest in their interpretations of the Quran and Hadith in several key ways:

**1. Succession of Leadership:**

*   **Historical Context:** The primary historical divergence between Sunni and Shia Muslims stems from disagreements over the rightful successor to Prophet Muhammad after his death in 632 CE. [2, 4, 8, 12] [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)
*   **Sunni View:** Sunni Muslims believed that leadership should be determined by consensus (Ijma) among the Muslim community, leading to the selection of Abu Bakr as the first caliph. [2, 4, 5] They accept the legitimacy of the first four caliphs. [4]
*   **Shia View:** Shia Muslims, on the other hand, maintain that Ali ibn Abi Talib, Muhammad's cousin and son-in-law, was divinely designated as his successor. [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [2, 4, 5, 6] They believe the leadership (Imamate) should have remained within the Prophet's family. [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [2, 5]

**2. Interpretation of Religious Authority:**

*   **Sunni Islam:** Emphasizes the authority of the elected caliphs and community consensus. [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [4, 5] Sunni thought is guided by four major schools of jurisprudence, which shape their interpretations of Islamic law. [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [4] Sunni religious scholars exert less authority over their followers compared to their Shia counterparts. [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [7] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)
*   **Shia Islam:** Upholds the Imamate, asserting that Ali and his descendants were divinely chosen to lead and possess special spiritual and political authority. [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [4, 6] Shia Muslims consider sayings attributed to the Prophet's family (Ahl al-Bayt) as authoritative. [4] They believe that the Imam is sinless and his authority is infallible because it comes directly from God. [5] Experienced Shia scholars (ayatollahs) have wide interpretative authority. [7] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)

**3. The Role of the Imams:**

*   **Shia View:** Imams are considered the sacred source of faith and moral guidance and have special authority in the interpretation of faith. [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [11] They are seen as successors of the Prophet Muhammad. [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [thecollector](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-13) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [11] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)
*   **Sunni View:** Sunnis do not believe in the concept of Imam in the same way as Shias. [11] They choose leaders of their religious communities. [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [11] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)

**4. Hadith Collections and Interpretation:**

*   **Different Collections:** While both Sunni and Shia Muslims consider the Quran divine, they have different opinions on the Hadith and favor different collections. [12, 15] Shia Muslims have their own Hadith collections and often differ on which Hadiths they accept as authentic. [11] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)
*   **Authenticity:** Shia scholars do not reject Sunni Hadith books completely but investigate every individual Hadith for authenticity, whether recorded by Shia or Sunni scholars. [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [10] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)
*   **Emphasis:** Sunni Muslims strictly follow the Quran and authentic Hadith collections, emphasizing unity through traditional Sharia. [3] Shia Muslims place greater emphasis on the teachings and interpretations of the Imams. [6]

**5. Practices and Rituals:**

*   **Distinct Rituals:** Distinct rituals mark the two sects. [4] Shia Muslims integrate practices like Taqiyyah (concealment of faith) and commemorate historical events like Karbala with unique rituals, including self-flagellation. [3] [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10)
*   **Commemoration:** Shias commemorate Ashura with public mourning to honor Husayn's martyrdom, while Sunnis observe it as a day of fasting to commemorate Moses' victory over Pharaoh. [4] [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)

**6. Key Theological Concepts:**

*   **Sunni Islam:** The Six Articles of Faith are Tawhid, Malaikah, Kutub, Nubuwwah, Akhirah, and Al-Qadr. [14]
*   **Shia Islam:** The Five Roots of Usul ad-Din are Tawhid, Adalat, Nubuwwah, Imamah, and Ma'ad. [14] They also emphasize social justice. [11] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)

**7. Quranic Interpretation:**

*   **Differing Approaches:** Shias derive the meaning of Quranic verses based on the teachings of the Prophet's progeny and loyal companions, while Sunnis rely on the teachings of the Prophet's companions. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [9] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)

**8. The Mahdi:**

*   **Differing Views:** While Shia and Sunnis differ on the nature of the Mahdi, many members of both groups believe that the Mahdi will appear at the end of the world to bring about a perfect and just Islamic society. [15] In Shia Islam, the Mahdi symbol has developed into a powerful and central religious idea. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [15] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)

**Shared Beliefs:**

Despite these differences, it is important to note that Sunni and Shia Muslims share core beliefs, including the oneness of Allah and the prophethood of Muhammad. [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [2, 3] Both accept the Five Pillars of Islam: Shahada, Salat, Zakat, Sawm, and Hajj. [5, 11, 15] [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2)


--- Research Result 6 ---
The main differences in the Hadith collections used by Sunni and Shia Muslims, and how these differences affect their legal and theological interpretations, can be summarized as follows:

**1. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [hadith](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-1) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-2) Different Hadith Collections:**

*   **Sunni:** Sunni Muslims primarily rely on six major Hadith collections, known as the *Kutub al-Sittah* or *al-Sihah al-Sitta* ("The Authentic Six"). [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-3) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-4) These are:
    *   *Sahih al-Bukhari* [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-3) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-2) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [almuslih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-5) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-6) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-4) [al-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-7)
    *   *Sahih Muslim* [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-3) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-2) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-4) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-8) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [hadith](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-1) [almuslih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-5) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-9)
    *   *Sunan Abu Dawood* [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-3) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-4) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0)
    *   *Sunan al-Tirmidhi* [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-4)
    *   *Sunan al-Nasa'i* [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [almuslih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-5) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-4)
    *   *Sunan Ibn Majah* [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-3) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-4) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-2) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-8) [almuslih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-5)
    *   Some include *Muwatta Imam Malik*, *Sunan al-Darimi*, and *Musnad Ahmad* in a list of nine hadith books.
*   **Shia:** Shia Muslims have their own distinct collections. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-10) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [hadith](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-9) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-11) The most important are the "Four Books" (*al-Kutub al-Arba'a*):
    *   *Al-Kafi* by Muhammad ibn Ya'qub al-Kulayni [brill](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-12) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [hadith](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-1)
    *   *Man La Yahduruhu al-Faqih* by Shaykh Saduq [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-11) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [hadith](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-1) [almuslih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-5)
    *   *Tahdhib al-Ahkam* by Shaykh Tusi [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [almuslih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-5)
    *   *Al-Istibsar* by Shaykh Tusi [brill](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-12) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [hadith](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-1)
    *   Other collections include *Wasail al-Shi'ah* and *Bihar al-Anwar*. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-11) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [hadith](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-1)

**2. [proceedingsiches](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-13) Differing Views on the Authority and Content of Hadith:**

*   **Sunni:**
    *   Hadith is second to the Quran as a source of Islamic law and guidance. [proceedingsiches](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-13)
    *   Emphasize the *Sunnah* (the traditions and practices of Muhammad). [umaryland](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-14) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15)
    *   Authenticity of a Hadith relies on a continuous and unbroken chain of narrators (***sanad***) tracing back to the Prophet Muhammad. [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16)
    *   Generally accept the narrations from the Prophet's companions (Sahaba).
*   **Shia:**
    *   Also consider Hadith important but place greater emphasis on the teachings and interpretations of their Imams, especially those from the *Ahl al-Bayt* (the Prophet's family). [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-17)
    *   Require the chain of narrators to trace back to the Prophet and the infallible Imams. [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-18)
    *   May reject Sunni Hadith if not also recorded in Shia sources or if the narrators are deemed unreliable due to their opposition to Ali or support of his enemies.
    *   Believe the Imams are divinely inspired and designated interpreters of law and theology. [umaryland](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-14)
    *   The sayings of the *Ahl al-Bayt*, even if not directly attributed to Muhammad, are considered Hadith. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15)

**3. Impact on Legal and Theological Interpretations:**

*   **Legal Interpretation:**
    *   **Sunni:** Sunni jurisprudence relies on the Quran, Hadith, *qiyas* (analogy), *ijma* (consensus). [umaryland](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-14) There are four main Sunni schools of law (*madhabs*) which offer alternative interpretations of legal decisions. [umaryland](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-14) [thelegallock](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-19) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0)
    *   **Shia:** Shia jurisprudence also uses the Quran and Hadith but gives significant weight to the interpretations of the Imams. [thelegallock](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-19) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-17) Shia legal interpretation allows more space for human reasoning (*ijtihad*). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0)
*   **Theological Differences:**
    *   **Sunni:** Believe that the caliphs should be chosen by a council. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15)
    *   **Shia:** Believe that Muhammad had named Ali ibn Abi Talib as his successor. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15) They believe in the doctrine of the Imamate, where certain individuals from Muhammad's family have special spiritual and political authority. [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-17)
    *   These differences extend to beliefs about the Mahdi (the prophesied redeemer of Islam) and practices such as *mut'ah* (temporary marriage), which is permitted in Twelver Shia Islam but not in Sunni Islam. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15)
    *   Different understandings of core beliefs. [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-17) [proceedingsiches](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-13) [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15) Shia Muslims have belief in Imamate and Justice as articles of belief, whereas Sunni have Hajj and Salat (prayer) in its place. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-8)

**4. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-11) Reliability of Hadith:**

*   **Sunni View:** Generally consider the *Sahih Bukhari* and *Sahih Muslim* as the most authentic Hadith collections. [almuslih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-5)
*   **Shia View:** While acknowledging that Sunni Hadith books contain some sound traditions, they also believe they contain weak and fabricated traditions. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-18) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-10) [hadith](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-1) They emphasize the importance of examining the authenticity of each Hadith individually. [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-9)

**5. Methodologies for Establishing Validity:**

*   **Sunni:** One condition for the authenticity of a Hadith is that its chain of transmission (*sanad*) must be continuous and unbroken back to the Prophet Muhammad. [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16)
*   **Shia:** Requires the authenticity of Hadith to be traced back to the Prophet and the infallible Imams without interruption, relying on the *Ahlul Bayt* lineage. [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16)

In conclusion, the distinct Hadith collections and differing methodologies for assessing their reliability contribute to significant variations in legal and theological interpretations between Sunni and Shia Islam. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-8) These differences, rooted in historical disagreements over leadership and authority, continue to shape the religious practices and beliefs of the two communities. [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-17) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15)

Imam pertama adalah Ali bin Abi Thalib, diikuti oleh Hasan dan Husain (cucu Nabi), dan seterusnya hingga Imam ke-12, Muhammad al-Mahdi, yang diyakini berada dalam keadaan gaib dan akan kembali pada akhir zaman [neliti](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGkVLg4OUEAdMm8MBdTMotdcFxI1VhRbQ6EwE9qlGfyvoAoZds3PM5YQfX2EjbW8UVERRHKO8-fFuszz-lmAjo16iPkL1gNC2dVlqFKJwuNATbfO2hUbCn1f9a_wJKPhPrgg_yIWn6vyy6mJYS4ycf37XF5El4r2TlxqUxNHYrKf35i8WjGKbKjK59l7xrV_cBhmpmMDPfv5mdzbr8w) [biblehub](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFRQ3ufZOXfpU0Vw16nmEHvsWzAyMwq4nlFer0i2aHm-ttiBePSvT4ue5Gg4odFCPJ6zUyW49GdcnmqbnGO6FDxHHltmSdNMfdovvmF1tub62rI9M6n5eMPSQLtMFMx2O9lmcsVGQKbUGPjSmKC7PiB8G3ygmAol60=).\n*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Tidak percaya bahwa Imamah ditunjuk secara ilahi. Mereka percaya bahwa setiap keturunan Ali (Alid) dapat menjadi Imam jika dia bangkit melawan ketidakadilan [iuqibogor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHjEYtXTmLVNRO-0O6GyfJcytOCuiRRUUBSAJrxtGL9iiR51NXW6GZYrkqE6-OKkz_zArlKfndM9RYWeUTTe6FEwSXhDID2KCdVStYuG6wYCjTo-EGOd4nh73wNDjJkOWVuFeJE5AF9rVTxz1DC0TK9a3HkjnxFPJHZQysWhpjIsYUynZa0x69h). Tidak seperti Itsna'asyariyah, Zaidiyah tidak meyakini kemaksuman Imam. Setelah Imam Ali, Imam Hasan, Imam Husain, Imam Ali Zainal Abidin, dan Zaid bin Ali, tanggung jawab imamah diemban oleh laki-laki dari keturunan Fatimah yang memenuhi kriteria: menyeru umat untuk mengakui ke-imamahannya, adil secara dhahir, alim, pemberani, dan dibaiat oleh orang-orang mukmin untuk berjihad [wikishia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQEJO5-hTpcLsNAXgAjopRFDfIJPzRTZ6waBnAT6H-3f3Z1B-pn929YMOtcxi1YUCXBSO317h_oTQtihyZ6laVWeZYHNSzwph7R9t0qyfHZ0pSIsWTkR1KKyL9VeJL8tm2E=).\n\n**2. Konsep Imamah:**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Tidak memiliki konsep Imamah seperti dalam Syiah. Pemimpin dipilih berdasarkan kemampuan dan dukungan komunitas.\n*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Imam memiliki otoritas spiritual yang setara dengan Nabi dan merupakan penafsir agama yang tidak mungkin salah. Imam diangkat secara ilahi dan maksum [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFX3Exm29aRfPy3bZWmwtIMlT4-YkbrXEkrUuRB46K6UB24XHnevLJxYzqMOL7WDxTu_4B_A4MqFijlslcYr5whTeoM7OztrK4Dszn24CTIqtUgtXSyeMplVGQ5e_iOcn5D_gFNJV0y6oD2Ogt5f2AKtS6LB9ZXn63QboPHR4cMvfbtcayNHpd1c0BXnk48wj3fzRue9RJbJX-sNR0run--aW_rgZmOBjKn).\n*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Imam adalah pemimpin yang saleh dan berani yang bangkit melawan ketidakadilan, tetapi mereka tidak harus maksum atau ditunjuk secara ilahi.\n\n**3. Sumber Hukum:**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Menggunakan Al-Quran dan Hadis (perkataan dan perbuatan Nabi Muhammad SAW) yang diriwayatkan oleh para sahabat Nabi secara luas [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFX3Exm29aRfPy3bZWmwtIMlT4-YkbrXEkrUuRB46K6UB24XHnevLJxYzqMOL7WDxTu_4B_A4MqFijlslcYr5whTeoM7OztrK4Dszn24CTIqtUgtXSyeMplVGQ5e_iOcn5D_gFNJV0y6oD2Ogt5f2AKtS6LB9ZXn63QboPHR4cMvfbtcayNHpd1c0BXnk48wj3fzRue9RJbJX-sNR0run--aW_rgZmOBjKn) [tempo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbDyQnBXyR8sVNwbvY1-Z8XRNKbZ_-M-tZSockappnSaqoWCHeDYrCKuvzrBWzSiy48ZkcV5bqrm8MeI44gpkpA6WD1BdVFNHjP_CT9h8c4r9xr2EY2EQhfWZq8juIaGnxDW9o47txJ3qZOxl8hq6kT2EYAa3a9yq5Yb05hlm2hLMLIOM=).\n*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Menggunakan Al-Quran dan Hadis yang diriwayatkan oleh Ahlul Bait (keluarga Nabi), yaitu Ali, Fatimah, Hasan, Husain, dan keturunan mereka.\n*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Menggunakan Al-Quran, Hadis, dan akal (rasionalisme) dalam menetapkan hukum. Mereka tidak membatasi penerimaan hadis hanya dari keluarga Nabi, tetapi juga menerima riwayat dari sahabat Nabi lainnya [tempo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbDyQnBXyR8sVNwbvY1-Z8XRNKbZ_-M-tZSockappnSaqoWCHeDYrCKuvzrBWzSiy48ZkcV5bqrm8MeI44gpkpA6WD1BdVFNHjP_CT9h8c4r9xr2EY2EQhfWZq8juIaGnxDW9o47txJ3qZOxl8hq6kT2EYAa3a9yq5Yb05hlm2hLMLIOM=).\n\n**4. Pandangan terhadap Sahabat Nabi:**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Menghormati semua sahabat Nabi Muhammad SAW dan menganggap mereka sebagai orang-orang yang adil dan dapat dipercaya.\n*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Beberapa kelompok Syiah Imamiyah dan Ismailiyah memiliki pandangan yang sangat kritis terhadap para sahabat Nabi yang tidak mendukung Ali sebagai khalifah pertama.\n*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Memiliki pandangan yang lebih lunak terhadap para sahabat Nabi [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGgD8Z09Osj7rwy2UB6-dDgUMfDJdvs125DXbBEDbP_ShDHIrYvy69nPuvJVUS64XGh80z1LHKt_0XRhAaiXbTZkMNHew5cCP2EA9lmS1-O1GtWaz7Tzlj_NRZZ6Z5Ofk_bbefioP0x5iL77VhOgdqtX2d4ehueb_Ce0H5eZJVLdwx2Y6yQf9bXRwJNhRuW-Gx6aRKZcGgTQoXb43VP). Mereka mengakui Abu Bakar, Umar, dan Utsman sebagai khalifah yang sah, meskipun mereka meyakini bahwa Ali lebih utama [tempo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbDyQnBXyR8sVNwbvY1-Z8XRNKbZ_-M-tZSockappnSaqoWCHeDYrCKuvzrBWzSiy48ZkcV5bqrm8MeI44gpkpA6WD1BdVFNHjP_CT9h8c4r9xr2EY2EQhfWZq8juIaGnxDW9o47txJ3qZOxl8hq6kT2EYAa3a9yq5Yb05hlm2hLMLIOM=).\n\n**5. Taqiyyah (Disimulasi):**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Tidak mengenal konsep taqiyyah dalam keadaan normal.\n*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Membolehkan taqiyyah (menyamarkan keyakinan) untuk melindungi diri dari penganiayaan.\n*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Menolak taqiyyah.\n\n**6. Keyakinan Tambahan:**\n\n*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Memiliki rukun iman yang disebut Ushuluddin, yang terdiri dari Tauhid (keesaan Allah), Adl (keadilan Allah), Nubuwwah (kenabian), Imamah (kepemimpinan), dan Ma'ad (hari kebangkitan) [jurnal-maarifinstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQEhZqsUZ29UsslLrEymGPwzN22F_dIdL7yQ5-KEh3sxC5EXD23dNbQ5TKJbprLquXhkENmAiF5VPsqCoGAr6lfuClO6eAr0eoBhhO5M1A2kXEEu7h0zv1_TLzTwL6qMM0erd0mQwrAjaFmYIXrDoj3TUjcvNXMtwywymFZHCs5Ej_VQREwOeRZcapk=).\n*   **Sunni:** Rukun Iman ada 6 (enam) :Iman kepada Allah, Iman kepada Malaikat-malaikat Nya, Iman kepada Kitab-kitab Nya, Iman kepada Rasul Nya, Iman kepada Yaumil Akhir / hari kiamat, Iman kepada Qadar, baik-buruknya dari Allah [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF8mUGgP_k5tVOMi-SY2mY7T-X6ELM2YKfQ1fFjmfvfEzzWioOlhJf9uUwuMVk4LxLd_8SgMQnHzxZOx2l8nh6D8sJ-7Vxpd6bXxRLKg_u6PzsmUipHN98W2HvV6uQhgcObfEwX0WzPlMFfARvGlhUQVMmKUFJZupFzz4aWPPeMFT2X7P16ZoFi_PSlQzQ05KELlWQuABxAq5bMQTWOVESO8HD6-g==).\n*   **Syiah:** Rukun Islam Syiah juga ada 5 (lima) tapi berbeda: a) As-Sholah, b) As-Shoum, c) Az-Zakah, d) Al-Haj, e) Al wilayah [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF8mUGgP_k5tVOMi-SY2mY7T-X6ELM2YKfQ1fFjmfvfEzzWioOlhJf9uUwuMVk4LxLd_8SgMQnHzxZOx2l8nh6D8sJ-7Vxpd6bXxRLKg_u6PzsmUipHN98W2HvV6uQhgcObfEwX0WzPlMFfARvGlhUQVMmKUFJZupFzz4aWPPeMFT2X7P16ZoFi_PSlQzQ05KELlWQuABxAq5bMQTWOVESO8HD6-g==).\n\n**7. Penyebaran Geografis:**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Merupakan mayoritas Muslim di sebagian besar dunia.\n*   **Syiah Itsna'asyariyah:** Mayoritas di Iran, Azerbaijan, Irak, dan Bahrain [fanack](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHpX0Bsv_hpMBbofU4Do9YaaVUYo5obM8SC0zLMsYexuue49DXe9o6AvLJ0IanUDAoCq8s17di-hZOKmR03aS2-ROt8xb9uKv2YAx63TJbn84sXE3GZddbuUuvnUjiIrKuMwxjIST_Ed7l3_xR4ElchxDnQ7SJd-44wJz8uh3oXFULZzo4GoQEEXeCYU2HuP4-5Oe9wGo4Y4-L0bmOVkPD6-U7y_1ydl-fC) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGgD8Z09Osj7rwy2UB6-dDgUMfDJdvs125DXbBEDbP_ShDHIrYvy69nPuvJVUS64XGh80z1LHKt_0XRhAaiXbTZkMNHew5cCP2EA9lmS1-O1GtWaz7Tzlj_NRZZ6Z5Ofk_bbefioP0x5iL77VhOgdqtX2d4ehueb_Ce0H5eZJVLdwx2Y6yQf9bXRwJNhRuW-Gx6aRKZcGgTQoXb43VP).     "The Sunni and Shia branches of Islam, while sharing core beliefs, differ in legal and ritual practices, particularly concerning prayer, marriage, and inheritance. These differences stem from historical and political disagreements, as well as varying interpretations of Islamic law (Sharia). [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)\n\n### Prayer [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)\n\n*   **Frequency:** Sunni Muslims typically pray five times a day at five distinct times, while Shia Muslims may combine certain prayers, praying three times a day (combining the noon and afternoon prayers, as well as the evening and night prayers). [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)\n*   **Physical Postures:** During prayer, Sunni Muslims often place their hands on their chest or stomach in the standing position, whereas Shia Muslims usually keep their hands at their sides. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)\n*   **Prostration:** Shia Muslims often place a small piece of clay or soil (turba) on the ground to prostrate on during their prayers, a practice not common among Sunni Muslims.\n*   **Recitation:** While both groups recite the opening chapter of the Quran (Al-Fatiha), there may be variations in additional supplications and phrases included in their prayers.\n*   **Intercession:** Major groups of Sunnis do not accept intercession. [calloflove](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4) Shia Muslims believe intercessory prayers can be made to Muhammad, his daughter Fatima, and the Twelve Imams. [calloflove](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4)\n\n### Marriage [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3) [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)\n\n*   **Witnesses:** Sunni marriages require two adult male witnesses at the time of the Nikah (marriage contract). [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) Shia marriages do not require witnesses at the time of the Nikah but require them at the time of divorce. [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)\n*   **Guardianship:** In Sunni law, there is a long list of guardians for marriage besides the father and grandfather. [lawnotes](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6) Under Shia law, only the father and grandfather can act as legal guardians (Wali-ul-nikah).\n*   **Marriage Types:** Sunni law divides marriages into valid, invalid, and irregular (voidable) marriages, while Shia law recognizes only valid or void marriages. [lawcolumn](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7)\n*   **Temporary Marriage (Mut'ah):** Shia Muslims believe in Nikah al-Mut'ah (temporary marriage), which is a fixed-term marriage contract that can be renewed, but automatically dissolves once the contract expires. [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) Sunni Muslims do not recognize this type of marriage. [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) Some Sunnis have Nikah-e-Misyar, which is a non-traditional temporary marriage contract, but both Sunni and Shia Muslims disagree over Nikah al Mut'ah and Nikah e Misyar. [muslimmarriagebureaugujarat](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)\n*   **Inter-sect Marriage:** It is permissible for a Shi'ite man to marry a Sunni girl if he is from among the moderate Shi'a groups. [dar-alifta](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-8) However, marriage between a Sunni and a Shi'ite is subject to environmental, social, and intellectual considerations. [dar-alifta](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-8)\n\n### Inheritance [wassiyyah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9) [islamicwillstrust](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10)\n\n*   **Classification of Heirs:** The root of the differing Sunni and Shia interpretations of inheritance law lies in heirs' fundamental classification. [pravasitax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-11)\n*   **Exclusion of Heirs:** Under Sunni law, the nearest in degree will exclude those related to a deceased by more remote. [wassiyyah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9) Shiaa follows the same, but the outcome of this rule is quite different.\n*   **Presence of Daughters:** The Sunni rules allow the Full Brothers or Paternal Brothers to inherit in Daughters' presence, but Shia law completely excludes Full or Paternal Brothers and Paternal Sisters in the presence of Daughters. [wassiyyah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9)\n*   **Non-Muslim Inheritors:** Sunni and Shia laws differ in their interpretations and applications of Non-Muslim inheritors. [wassiyyah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9) [ipleaders](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-12)\n*   **Distribution:** Sunni law follows the Quranic Law which is the amalgamation of the old customary Law, whereas Shia refuses to believe saying that this law was not endorsed by the Quran itself and therefore new laws must be introduced. [islamicwillstrust](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10)\n*   **Heirs:** Sunni law has three classes of heirs: sharers, residuaries, and distant kindred. Shia law has two classes of heirs: shares and residuaries. [ipleaders](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-12)\n*   **Doctrine of Primogeniture:** The doctrine of primogeniture is not recognized in Sunni law. [lawnotes](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6) The doctrine of primogeniture is recognized in Shia law.\n*   **Per Capita vs. Per Stirpes Distribution:** Under Sunni law, if a person dies leaving three grandsons by a predeceased son and two grandsons by another predeceased son, all five grandsons will inherit the property in equal shares each taking 1/5th share (Per Capita distribution). [pravasitax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-11) Under Shia law, the three children of one predeceased son take 1/2 and other 1/2 goes to the two children of the predeceased son (Per Stirpes distribution). [pravasitax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-11)\n\nIt is important to note that both Sunni and Shia Muslims share the same fundamental beliefs and practices of Islam, including the five pillars. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) The Quran does not explicitly mention Shia or Sunni Islam because the division occurred after its revelation. [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-13) The divisions that arose between them are historical and political rather than religiously mandated. [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-13)\n",
    "The theological differences between Sunni and Shia Islam manifest in their interpretations of the Quran and Hadith in several key ways:\n\n**1. Succession of Leadership:**\n\n*   **Historical Context:** The primary historical divergence between Sunni and Shia Muslims stems from disagreements over the rightful successor to Prophet Muhammad after his death in 632 CE. [2, 4, 8, 12] [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)\n*   **Sunni View:** Sunni Muslims believed that leadership should be determined by consensus (Ijma) among the Muslim community, leading to the selection of Abu Bakr as the first caliph. [2, 4, 5] They accept the legitimacy of the first four caliphs. [4]\n*   **Shia View:** Shia Muslims, on the other hand, maintain that Ali ibn Abi Talib, Muhammad's cousin and son-in-law, was divinely designated as his successor. [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [2, 4, 5, 6] They believe the leadership (Imamate) should have remained within the Prophet's family. [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [2, 5]\n\n**2. Interpretation of Religious Authority:**\n\n*   **Sunni Islam:** Emphasizes the authority of the elected caliphs and community consensus. [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [4, 5] Sunni thought is guided by four major schools of jurisprudence, which shape their interpretations of Islamic law. [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [4] Sunni religious scholars exert less authority over their followers compared to their Shia counterparts. [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [7] [crestresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [cfr](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [learnreligions](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [eurasiareview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [explore-islam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [Current time information in Manyu, CM](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [duaholyquran](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [worldhistoryedu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)\n*   **Shia Islam:** Upholds the Imamate, asserting that Ali and his descendants were divinely chosen to lead and possess special spiritual and political authority. [proceedingsiches](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-13) Differing Views on the Authority and Content of Hadith:**\n\n*   **Sunni:**\n    *   Hadith is second to the Quran as a source of Islamic law and guidance. [proceedingsiches](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-13)\n    *   Emphasize the *Sunnah* (the traditions and practices of Muhammad). [umaryland](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-14) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15)\n    *   Authenticity of a Hadith relies on a continuous and unbroken chain of narrators (***sanad***) tracing back to the Prophet Muhammad. [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16)\n    *   Generally accept the narrations from the Prophet's companions (Sahaba).\n*   **Shia:**\n    *   Also consider Hadith important but place greater emphasis on the teachings and interpretations of their Imams, especially those from the *Ahl al-Bayt* (the Prophet's family). [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-17)\n    *   Require the chain of narrators to trace back to the Prophet and the infallible Imams. [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-18)\n    *   May reject Sunni Hadith if not also recorded in Shia sources or if the narrators are deemed unreliable due to their opposition to Ali or support of his enemies.\n    *   Believe the Imams are divinely inspired and designated interpreters of law and theology. [umaryland](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-14)\n    *   The sayings of the *Ahl al-Bayt*, even if not directly attributed to Muhammad, are considered Hadith. Impact on Legal and Theological Interpretations:**\n\n*   **Legal Interpretation:**\n    *   **Sunni:** Sunni jurisprudence relies on the Quran, Hadith, *qiyas* (analogy), *ijma* (consensus). [umaryland](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-14) There are four main Sunni schools of law (*madhabs*) which offer alternative interpretations of legal decisions. [umaryland](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-14) [thelegallock](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-19) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0)\n    *   **Shia:** Shia jurisprudence also uses the Quran and Hadith but gives significant weight to the interpretations of the Imams. [thelegallock](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-19) [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-17) Shia legal interpretation allows more space for human reasoning (*ijtihad*). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0)\n*   **Theological Differences:**\n    *   **Sunni:** Believe that the caliphs should be chosen by a council. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15)\n    *   **Shia:** Believe that Muhammad had named Ali ibn Abi Talib as his successor. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-0) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15) They believe in the doctrine of the Imamate, where certain individuals from Muhammad's family have special spiritual and political authority. [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-17)\n    *   These differences extend to beliefs about the Mahdi (the prophesied redeemer of Islam) and practices such as *mut'ah* (temporary marriage), which is permitted in Twelver Shia Islam but not in Sunni Islam. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15)\n    *   Different understandings of core beliefs. [fiveable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-17) [proceedingsiches](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-13) [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-15) Shia Muslims have belief in Imamate and Justice as articles of belief, whereas Sunni have Hajj and Salat (prayer) in its place. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-8)\n\n**4. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-11) Reliability of Hadith:**\n\n*   **Sunni View:** Generally consider the *Sahih Bukhari* and *Sahih Muslim* as the most authentic Hadith collections. [almuslih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-5)\n*   **Shia View:** While acknowledging that Sunni Hadith books contain some sound traditions, they also believe they contain weak and fabricated traditions. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-18) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-10) [hadith](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-1) They emphasize the importance of examining the authenticity of each Hadith individually. [stackexchange](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-9)\n\n**5. Methodologies for Establishing Validity:**\n\n*   **Sunni:** One condition for the authenticity of a Hadith is that its chain of transmission (*sanad*) must be continuous and unbroken back to the Prophet Muhammad. [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16)\n*   **Shia:** Requires the authenticity of Hadith to be traced back to the Prophet and the infallible Imams without interruption, relying on the *Ahlul Bayt* lineage. [ijor](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-16)\n\nIn conclusion, the distinct Hadith collections and differing methodologies for assessing their reliability contribute to significant variations in legal and theological interpretations between Sunni and Shia Islam. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/5-8) These differences, rooted in historical disagreements over leadership and authority, continue to shape the religious practices and beliefs of the two communities.
